< date>
1435693281219< /date>
< Rate>
4<//Rate>
<text>We put an ABS electric brake system with the remote accumulator in a street rod.  the pump and accumulator  failed after only about  1200 miles which IMO was related to design issues.   ABS offered a replacement (updated) pump and accumulator at a significantly reduced price to replace the original units.  So far the updated system has performed flawlessly.  Regarding servicing this system there is an "O" ring that is placed between the accumulator and the pump body.  Care must be taken not to damage that "O" ring and insure it is evenly compressed when tightening the accumulator.   When operating correctly this system is a good solution for a frame mounted M/C.   Both Pedro and Memo were very helpful in correcting the problem and offering a reasonable settlement for the failure.< /text>< Pictures>

<user_name>specopspilot</user_name>< time>
1443514478334< /time>
< Rate>
2</Rate>
<review>Basically they make there own brackets and then just take other rotors and calipers from other cars and sell it as a kit. While this is smart for them, should you need break pads or seals or whatever you can't go to the auto parts store and get them, because you don't know what year make and model car they are from. The break booster hit a support on my car and they told me "just remove the support". I had to end up removing the proportioning valve, mount it elsewhere and make new break lines to connect the two. Either that or "remove a SUPPORT off my classic car. So the direct bolt on kit isn't quite so direct bolt on. The calipers need painting or they will rust like mine did (didn't say to do that anywhere) The instructions are horrible, the picture isn't clear enough to show how the stuff bolts together, the how to steps are not even close to complete. So if you are a figure it out kind of person you are good cause you're going to have to just figure it out,  if not you're SOL.There are no torque specs....remember this is a drum to disk conversion I can't just look in my OEM book for torque specks. My break lines leak at the caliper, afraid to tighten them any more and break the bolt because there are no torque specs...the old guy that answers the phone is rude and it took way longer to get in than I was quoted (didn't tell me they were back ordered) I wouldn't use there services again. I forget why I chose them over Wilwod to start with. The truck I'm building now and every future build will not have a ABS part on them.</review>< Pics>

<gmap_id>0x80c29c1878b9d283:0x963a6d8b2ed60c78< /gmap_id><date>1575156434537< /date>< review>
Massis Kabob offers Middle Eastern cuisine in the food court of the Westfield Topanga Mall. They have a few beef kabob dishes, a couple with fish: trout and tilapia, as well as a lamb dish. Most all come with basmati rice and a side of what is often referred to as Israeli salad (cucumbers and tomatoes). So, the rice is generally good, the meats however can be dry and often have charring from the grill. Some don't like that, but it is at least properly grilled. Prices are moderate, certainly higher than what you'd pay for cheaper fast food options. Service is okay.<//review>

< Review>
We purchased a car from this dealership yesterday, and it was without a doubt the WORST CAR BUYING EXPERIENCE EVER.  I want to say that I have bought a few cars but never left so disappointed as I did yesterday.  Rick was the sales associate, and my husband and I had already done some searching before we reached the lot and had two cars specifically in mind, we let Rick know this and he took us to the two cars we had inquired about.  After test driving and briefly discussing the two cars we decided that we wanted to purchase a car from this dealer.  Rick took us into the lobby to have a seat and talk financing.  We started off by letting Rick know that we were already pre-approved by our own bank with a bankruptcy on our history at a rate of 3.99% so we asked him to start by running our information and seeing if they could beat the rate with a different bank since we knew they were part of the CUDL system.  Rick proceeded to inform us that "We like to see some kind of down payment with this kind of purchase, so what were you thinking? They like to see something like $4,000." We let him know that was not a problem if that was the route we took but again said that we would like him to just start by trying to beat the rate we had been pre-approved for.  He then goes into the office of a gentleman in charge of getting us pre-approved and after a few seconds comes back out with a print out with the break down of what we would be paying, how much our payment would be and so on.  I noticed at the top it had the same rate of 3.99% so I asked Rick, "Does that mean you guys couldn't beat the rate?" and he replies nonchalantly "We didn't even try..." so we review the print out and we ask him to make some adjustments, he takes the paperwork back and comes out with a new print out and we review it one more time at this point Rick asks, "Do we have a deal?" and I say "fill up the tank, wash the car and you have a deal."  Anyone who has bought a car before would think this is a reasonable offer BUT NO he comes back with, "We don't do that for used cars, only new ones because we can get reimbursed, and the car wash will be about thirty minutes."  We proceed with purchasing the car because we knew regardless of the service we were receiving this was still a good deal for the car we bought.  Mayra B. was great she was friendly, prompt and efficient.  She was the only good part of the whole experience. After we finished we were walked out to the car by Rick who at this point was extremely friendly (unlike before) and once we got to the car he did offer to go over some things about the car but we declined, and he once again asked us to take the time to at least activate our 3 month free trial of OnStar because if we don't he would hear it from GM, but we had already told him we were not interested.  Today I called Ray Tarelli who is the Sales Manager hoping that Ray would try to make it right but he did not express an ounce of empathy towards our experience yesterday.  He actually went so far as to say that it was our fault because we didn't let Rick do his job, when I asked what he meant he said, "Rick was trying to set up your OnStar and you wouldn't let him because you were in such a hurry."HE EVEN HUNG UP ON ME!!! We had already expressed that we were not interested in signing up for something we were never intending to use/purchase. This is not how you treat customers and I will never recommend this dealership to anyone.  Seek a car elsewhere!!!< /Review>
